REQUIREMENT:- DO NOT OPERATE EARLY Neutral Bay Junction (late night and early morning services)
* Services operating between approximately 24:30 (00:30) and 29:00 (05:00) must provide compulsory connections to route 144N at Neutral Bay, allowing passengers from City QVB to transfer to route 144N and for passengers from North Sydney to transfer from route 144N, and vice-versa in the opposite direction.
